    for link in result_links[:max_results]:\n            title = link.get_text(strip=True)\n            url = link.get(\'href\', \'\')\n            \n            # Get snippet from nearby elements\n Shorter timeout\n            \n            if result.returncode == 0:\n                results = result.stdout.strip().split(\'\\n\')\n                print(f"Found {len(results)} results")\n                \n                for i, result_line in enumerate(results, 1):\n                    if not result_line.strip():\n                        continue\n                    \n                    try:\n                        parts = result_line.split(\' | \')\n                        if len(parts) >= 4:\n                            title = parts[0]\n                            video_id = parts[1]\n                            upload_date = parts[2] if parts[2] != \'NA\' else \'\'\n                            uploader = parts[3] if parts[3] != \'NA\' else \'\'\n                            \n                            # Look for the downloaded file\n                                temp_files = [f for f in os.listdir(workspace_dir) if f.startswith(f\'temp_vid_{result["video_id"]}\')]\n                                \n                                if temp_files:\n                                    temp_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, temp_files[0])\n                                    \n                                    # Convert to JPG\n                                    convert_cmd = [\n                                        \'ffmpeg\',\n                                        \'-i\', temp_file,\n                                        \'-vframes\', \'1\',\n                                        \'-q:v\', \'2\',\n                                        \'-y\',\n                                        output_path\n                                    ]\n                                    \n                                    convert_result = subprocess.run(convert_cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)\n                                    \n                                    if convert_result.returncode == 0 and os.path.exists(output_path):\n                                        print(f"\\n*** SUCCESS! Clean up\n                                        os.remove(temp_file)\n                                        \n                                        # Save results\n                                        final_result = {\n                                            \'success\': True,\n                                            \'video_found\': result,\n                                            \'frame_extracted\': {\n                                                \'timestamp\': timestamp,\n                                                \'filename\': output_filename,\n                                                \'path\': output_path,\n                                                \'size_bytes\': os.path.getsize(output_path)\n                                            },\n                                            \'analysis_time\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n                                        }\n                                        \n                                        results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'mario_kart_success.json\')\n                                        with open(results_file, \'w\') as f:\n                                            json.dump(final_result, f, indent=2)\n                                        \n                                        print(f"\\n*** MISSION ACCOMPLISHED! ***")\n                                        print(f"Found GameGrumps Mario Kart video from May 14, 2017")\n                                        print(f"Extracted frame at 2:00 showing the racetrack")\n                                        print(f"Frame saved as: {output_filename}")\n                                        \n                                        break  #
